Here is the DFS algorithm:
```scss
function dfs(node):
    if node == V9:
        return True
    if node in visited:
        return False
    visited.add(node)
    for neighbor in neighbors(node):
        if dfs(neighbor):
            return True
    visited.remove(node)
    return False
```

```scss
else:

```
